
**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                                                                               | Description                                               |
| ------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------- |
| `params`      | `{ query: string; ftsWeight?: number; vecWeight?: number; graphWeight?: number; limit?: number; }` | Search parameters including query and optional mode/limit |
| `projectRoot` | `: string`                                                                                         | Optional project root path; defaults to resolved root     |

**Returns** — EngineResult with merged and ranked results from all search backends

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await memorySearchHybrid({ query: 'authentication flow' }, '/project');
```

## memoryGraphRemove(params, projectRoot)

Remove a node or edge from the PageIndex graph.

**Signature**

```typescript
(params: { nodeId?: string; fromId?: string; toId?: string; edgeType?: string; }, projectRoot?: string) => Promise<EngineResult>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                                                      | Description                                           |
| ------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------- |
| `params`      | `{ nodeId?: string; fromId?: string; toId?: string; edgeType?: string; }` | Parameters specifying the node or edge to remove      |
| `projectRoot` | `: string`                                                                | Optional project root path; defaults to resolved root |

**Returns** — EngineResult confirming the removal

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await memoryGraphRemove({ type: 'node', nodeId: 'stale-concept' }, '/project');
```

## coreTaskNext(projectRoot, params, , )

Suggest next task to work on based on priority, phase, age, and deps.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, params?: { count?: number; explain?: boolean; }) => Promise<{ suggestions: Array<{ id: string; title: string; priority: string; phase: string | null; score: number; reasons?: string[]; }>; totalCandidates: number; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                       | Description                                                            |
| ------------- | ------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                                   | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                       |
| `params`      | `: { count?: number; explain?: boolean; }` | Optional scoring configuration                                         |
| ``            | `string`                                   | params.count - Number of suggestions to return (default: 1)            |
| ``            | `string`                                   | params.explain - When true, include scoring reasons in each suggestion |

**Returns** — Ranked suggestions with scores and the total number of eligible candidates

**Example**

```typescript
const { suggestions } = await coreTaskNext('/project', { count: 3, explain: true });
console.log(suggestions[0].id, suggestions[0].score);
```

## coreTaskBlockers(projectRoot, params, , )

Show blocked tasks and analyze blocking chains.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, params?: { analyze?: boolean; limit?: number; }) => Promise<{ blockedTasks: Array<{ id: string; title: string; status: string; depends?: string[]; blockingChain: string[]; }>; criticalBlockers: BottleneckTask[]; summary: string; total: number; limit: number; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                       | Description                                                            |
| ------------- | ------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                                   | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                       |
| `params`      | `: { analyze?: boolean; limit?: number; }` | Optional analysis configuration                                        |
| ``            | `string`                                   | params.analyze - When true, compute transitive blocking chains         |
| ``            | `string`                                   | params.limit - Maximum number of blocked tasks to return (default: 20) |

**Returns** — Blocked tasks with optional blocking chains, critical bottleneck tasks, and a summary

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await coreTaskBlockers('/project', { analyze: true, limit: 10 });
```


## coreTaskRelatesAdd(projectRoot, taskId, relatedId, type, reason)

Add a relation between two tasks.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskId: string, relatedId: string, type: string, reason?: string) => Promise<{ from: string; to: string; type: string; reason?: string; added: boolean; }>
```

| Name          | Type       | Description                                               |
| ------------- | ---------- | --------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`   | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory          |

| `relatedId`   | `string`   | The target task ID to relate to                           |

| `reason`      | `: string` | Optional human-readable reason for the relation           |

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await coreTaskRelatesAdd('/project', 'T010', 'T020', 'related-to', 'Shared scope');

```

## coreTaskAnalyze(projectRoot, taskId, params, )

## coreTaskRestore(projectRoot, taskId, params, , )

Restore a cancelled task back to pending.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskId: string, params?: { cascade?: boolean; notes?: string; }) => Promise<{ task: string; restored: string[]; count: number; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                       | Description                                                                 |
| ------------- | ------------------------------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                                   | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                            |
| `taskId`      | `string`                                   | The cancelled task ID to restore                                            |
| `params`      | `: { cascade?: boolean; notes?: string; }` | Optional restore options                                                    |
| ``            | `string`                                   | params.cascade - When true, also restores cancelled child tasks recursively |
| ``            | `string`                                   | params.notes - Optional note appended to each restored task's notes array   |

**Returns** — The task ID, list of restored task IDs, and total count

**Example**


## coreTaskCancel(projectRoot, taskId, params, )

Cancel a task (sets status to 'cancelled', a soft terminal state). Use restore to reverse. Use delete for permanent removal.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskId: string, params?: { reason?: string; }) => Promise<{ task: string; cancelled: boolean; reason?: string; cancelledAt: string; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                     | Description                                                           |
| ------------- | ------------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                 | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                      |
| `taskId`      | `string`                 | The task ID to cancel                                                 |
| `params`      | `: { reason?: string; }` | Optional cancel options                                               |
| ``            | `string`                 | params.reason - Human-readable cancellation reason stored on the task |

**Returns** — Confirmation with cancelled flag and timestamp

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await coreTaskCancel('/project', 'T077', { reason: 'Superseded by T080' });
console.log(result.cancelledAt);
```

## coreTaskUnarchive(projectRoot, taskId, params, , )

Move an archived task back to active tasks.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskId: string, params?: { status?: string; preserveStatus?: boolean; }) => Promise<{ task: string; unarchived: boolean; title: string; status: string; }>
```

| Name          | Type                                               | Description                                                                  |
| ------------- | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                                           | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                             |
| `taskId`      | `string`                                           | The archived task ID to unarchive                                            |
| `params`      | `: { status?: string; preserveStatus?: boolean; }` | Optional unarchive options                                                   |
| ``            | `string`                                           | params.status - Target status for the restored task (default: "pending")     |
| ``            | `string`                                           | params.preserveStatus - When true, keeps the task's original archived status |

**Returns** — Confirmation with task ID, title, and resulting status

**Example**


**Example**

```typescript
const overview = await coreTaskDepsOverview('/project');
console.log(`${overview.blockedTasks.length} blocked, ${overview.readyTasks.length} ready`);
```

## coreTaskDepsCycles(projectRoot)

Detect circular dependencies across the project.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string) => Promise<{ hasCycles: boolean; cycles: Array<{ path: string[]; tasks: Array<Pick<TaskRef, "id" | "title">>; }>; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type     | Description                                      |
| ------------- | -------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| `projectRoot` | `string` | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory |

**Returns** — Whether cycles exist and the list of detected cycles with their task paths

**Example**

```typescript
const { hasCycles, cycles } = await coreTaskDepsCycles('/project');
if (hasCycles) console.log('Circular deps:', cycles.map(c => c.path.join(' -> ')));
```

## coreTaskDepends(projectRoot, taskId, direction, options, )

List dependencies for a task in a given direction.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskId: string, direction?: "upstream" | "downstream" | "both", options?: { tree?: boolean; }) => Promise<{ taskId: string; direction: string; upstream: TaskRef[]; downstream: TaskRef[]; unresolvedChain: number; leafBlockers: TaskRef[]; allDepsReady: boolean; hint?: string; upstreamTree?: FlatTreeNode[]; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                     | Description                                                                                                 |
| ------------- | ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                                 | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                                                            |
| `taskId`      | `string`                                 | The task ID to inspect                                                                                      |
| `direction`   | `: "upstream" \| "downstream" \| "both"` | Direction to traverse: "upstream" (what this task depends on), "downstream" (what depends on it), or "both" |
| `options`     | `: { tree?: boolean; }`                  | Optional display configuration                                                                              |
| ``            | `string`                                 | options.tree - When true, includes a recursive upstream dependency tree                                     |

**Returns** — Upstream and downstream deps, transitive chain length, leaf blockers, and readiness status

**Example**

```typescript
const deps = await coreTaskDepends('/project', 'T100', 'both', { tree: true });
console.log('Leaf blockers:', deps.leafBlockers.map(b => b.id));
```

## coreTaskStats(projectRoot, epicId)

Compute task statistics.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, epicId?: string) => Promise<{ total: number; pending: number; active: number; blocked: number; done: number; cancelled: number; byPriority: Record<string, number>; byType: Record<string, number>; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type       | Description                                      |
| ------------- | ---------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| `projectRoot` | `string`   | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory |
| `epicId`      | `: string` | Optional epic ID to scope stats to that subtree  |

**Returns** — Status counts, priority distribution, and type distribution

**Example**

```typescript
const stats = await coreTaskStats('/project', 'T001');
console.log(`${stats.done}/${stats.total} complete`);
```

## coreTaskExport(projectRoot, params, , , )

Export tasks as JSON or CSV.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, params?: { format?: "json" | "csv"; status?: string; parent?: string; }) => Promise<unknown>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                                                | Description                                                      |
| ------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`                                                            | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                 |
| `params`      | `: { format?: "json" \| "csv"; status?: string; parent?: string; }` | Optional export configuration                                    |
| ``            | `string`                                                            | params.format - Output format: "json" (default) or "csv"         |
| ``            | `string`                                                            | params.status - Filter to only tasks with this status            |
| ``            | `string`                                                            | params.parent - Filter to tasks under this parent ID (recursive) |

**Returns** — Export payload with format, content/tasks, and task count

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await coreTaskExport('/project', { format: 'csv', status: 'done' });
console.log(result.content); // CSV string
```

## coreTaskHistory(projectRoot, taskId, limit)

Get task history from the audit log.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskId: string, limit?: number) => Promise<Array<Record<string, unknown>>>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type       | Description                                                |
| ------------- | ---------- | ---------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`   | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory           |
| `taskId`      | `string`   | The task ID to retrieve history for                        |
| `limit`       | `: number` | Maximum number of history entries to return (default: 100) |

**Returns** — Array of audit log entries ordered by timestamp descending

**Example**

```typescript
const history = await coreTaskHistory('/project', 'T042', 10);
for (const entry of history) console.log(entry.timestamp, entry.operation);
```

## coreTaskLint(projectRoot, taskId)

**Signature**

```typescript

```

| Name          | Type       | Description                                      |
| ------------- | ---------- | ------------------------------------------------ |

## coreTaskBatchValidate(projectRoot, taskIds, checkMode)

Validate multiple tasks at once.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, taskIds: string[], checkMode?: "full" | "quick") => Promise<{ results: Record<string, Array<{ severity: "error" | "warning"; rule: string; message: string; }>>; summary: { totalTasks: number; validTasks: number; invalidTasks: number; totalIssues: number; errors: number; warnings: number; }; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                  | Description                                                                            |
| ------------- | --------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`              | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                                       |
| `taskIds`     | `string[]`            | Array of task IDs to validate                                                          |
| `checkMode`   | `: "full" \| "quick"` | Validation depth: "full" runs all checks, "quick" checks only title/description/status |

**Returns** — Per-task validation results and an aggregate summary with error/warning counts

**Example**

```typescript
const { summary } = await coreTaskBatchValidate('/project', ['T001', 'T002'], 'full');
console.log(`${summary.validTasks}/${summary.totalTasks} valid`);
```

## coreTaskImport(projectRoot, source, overwrite)

Import tasks from a JSON source string.

**Signature**

```typescript
(projectRoot: string, source: string, overwrite?: boolean) => Promise<{ imported: number; skipped: number; errors: string[]; remapTable?: Record<string, string>; }>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type        | Description                                                                  |
| ------------- | ----------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `projectRoot` | `string`    | Absolute path to the CLEO project root directory                             |
| `source`      | `string`    | JSON string containing an array of tasks or an object with a `tasks` array   |
| `overwrite`   | `: boolean` | When true, overwrites existing tasks with matching IDs; otherwise skips them |

**Returns** — Import summary with counts of imported, skipped, errors, and optional ID remap table

**Example**

```typescript
const json = JSON.stringify([{ id: 'T500', title: 'New task', status: 'pending', priority: 'medium' }]);
const result = await coreTaskImport('/project', json, false);
console.log(`Imported ${result.imported}, skipped ${result.skipped}`);
```

## runUpgrade(, , , , , , )

Run a full upgrade pass on the project .cleo/ directory.  Steps:   1. Pre-flight storage check (JSON → SQLite)   2. If migration needed and not dry-run, run auto-migration with backup   3. Schema version checks on JSON files   4. Structural repairs (checksums, missing fields)

**Signature**

```typescript
(options?: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }) => Promise<UpgradeResult>
```

**Parameters**

| Name | Type                                                                                                                                                        | Description                                                                |
| ---- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.dryRun  Preview changes without applying                           |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.includeGlobal  Also check global \~/.cleo                          |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.autoMigrate  Auto-migrate storage if needed (default: true)        |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.forceDetect  Force re-detection of project type (ignore staleness) |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.mapCodebase  Run full codebase analysis and store to brain.db      |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.projectName  Update project name in project-info and nexus         |
| ``   | `: { dryRun?: boolean; includeGlobal?: boolean; autoMigrate?: boolean; forceDetect?: boolean; mapCodebase?: boolean; projectName?: string; cwd?: string; }` | options.cwd  Project directory override                                    |

## diagnoseUpgrade()

Deep diagnostic inspection of schema and migration state.  Unlike bare `cleo upgrade` which skips checks that "look OK", --diagnose validates: - tasks.db: all required columns present via PRAGMA table\_info - tasks.db: migration journal entries match local migration files - brain.db: migration journal entries match local migration files - brain.db: expected tables exist - Stale/orphaned journal entries detected and reported  Read-only: does not modify any data.   T131

**Signature**

```typescript
(options?: { cwd?: string; }) => Promise<DiagnoseResult>
```

## VerificationGate

Main Verification Gate class  Orchestrates 4-layer validation and determines pass/fail status. Each layer must pass before proceeding to the next.

**Signature**

```typescript
typeof VerificationGate
```

**Methods**

### verifyOperation()

Execute all 4 gate layers sequentially  Stops at first failure unless in advisory mode.

```typescript
(context: OperationContext) => Promise<VerificationResult>
```

### runLayer()

Run a single validation layer with timing

```typescript
(layer: GateLayer, validator: () => Promise<LayerResult>) => Promise<LayerResult>
```

### buildSuccessResult()

Build success result when all gates pass

```typescript
(layers: Record<GateLayer, LayerResult>) => VerificationResult
```

### buildFailureResult()

Build failure result when a gate fails

```typescript
(layers: Record<GateLayer, LayerResult>, blockedAt: GateLayer) => VerificationResult
```

### determineSemanticExitCode()

Determine semantic layer exit code from violations

```typescript
(violations: GateViolation[]) => ProtocolExitCode
```

### determineReferentialExitCode()

Determine referential layer exit code from violations

```typescript
(violations: GateViolation[]) => ProtocolExitCode
```

### determineProtocolExitCode()

Determine protocol layer exit code from violations

```typescript
(violations: GateViolation[]) => ProtocolExitCode
```

### requiresValidation()

Check if an operation requires gate validation  All mutate operations require validation. Query operations skip validation for performance.

```typescript
(context: OperationContext) => boolean
```

### getLayerName()

Get human-readable layer name

```typescript
(layer: GateLayer) => string
```

## createVerificationGate()

Factory function for creating verification gates

**Signature**

```typescript
(strictMode?: boolean) => VerificationGate
```

## WorkflowGateTracker

WorkflowGateTracker  Tracks the status of all 6 workflow verification gates for a task. Implements Section 7.4 failure cascade behavior: when a gate fails, all downstream gates reset to null.   T3141

**Signature**

```typescript
typeof WorkflowGateTracker
```

**Methods**

### getGateStatus()

Get the status of a specific gate

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName) => WorkflowGateStatus
```

### getGateState()

Get the full state of a specific gate

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName) => WorkflowGateState | undefined
```

### getAllGates()

Get all gate states

```typescript
() => WorkflowGateState[]
```

### canAttempt()

Check if a gate can be attempted (all dependencies passed)

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName) => boolean
```

### passGate()

Mark a gate as passed.

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName, agent?: string) => boolean
```

### failGate()

Mark a gate as failed.  Per Section 7.4: When a gate fails, all downstream gates reset to null.

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName, reason?: string) => boolean
```

### cascadeReset()

Reset a gate and all downstream gates to null.

```typescript
(failedGateName: WorkflowGateName) => void
```

### updateBlockedStatus()

Update blocked status for all gates based on current state.

```typescript
() => void
```

### allPassed()

Check if all gates have passed

```typescript
() => boolean
```

### getPendingGates()

Get all gates that are currently blocked or have null status

```typescript
() => WorkflowGateState[]
```

### getNextAttemptable()

Get the next gate that can be attempted

```typescript
() => WorkflowGateName | null
```

### getDownstreamGates()

Get downstream gates of a given gate (not including the gate itself)

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName) => WorkflowGateName[]
```

### toRecord()

Serialize gate states to a plain record

```typescript
() => Record<string, WorkflowGateStatus>
```

### fromRecord()

Restore gate states from a record

```typescript
(record: Record<string, WorkflowGateStatus>) => void
```

### isValidGate()

Check if a gate name is valid

```typescript
(gateName: WorkflowGateName) => boolean
```

## buildMcpInputSchema()

Build a JSON Schema `input_schema` object from an `OperationDef`.  Algorithm:  1. Iterate `def.params`  2. Skip params where schema `mcp.hidden === true`  3. Map ParamType → JSON Schema type  4. Collect names where `required === true` into `required[]`  5. Return  type: 'object', properties, required

**Signature**

```typescript
(def: OperationDef) => JSONSchemaObject
```

## buildCommanderArgs()

Split `OperationDef.params` into positional arguments and option flags, suitable for Commander.js registration.  - `cli.positional === true` → goes into `positionals[]` - everything else with a `cli` key → goes into `options[]` - Params with no `cli` key → dispatch-only; excluded from both arrays

**Signature**

```typescript
(def: OperationDef) => CommanderArgSplit
```

## buildCommanderOptionString()

Build the Commander option string for a single non-positional ParamDef.  Examples:    name:'taskId', type:'string', cli:      → '--taskId '    name:'status', type:'string', cli:short:'-s', flag:'status'      → '-s, --status '    name:'dryRun', type:'boolean', cli:flag:'dry-run'      → '--dry-run'    name:'limit', type:'number', cli:      → '--limit '

**Signature**

```typescript
(param: ParamDef) => string
```

## camelToKebab()

Convert a camelCase string to kebab-case. e.g. 'includeArchive' → 'include-archive'

**Signature**

```typescript
(s: string) => string
```

## validateRequiredParamsDef()

Validates that all required parameters are present in the request. Returns an array of missing parameter names.  Replaces the old `requiredParams: string[]` check in registry.ts.

**Signature**

```typescript
(def: OperationDef, params?: Record<string, unknown>) => string[]
```

## validateSchema(schemaType, data)

Validate data against a CLEO schema

**Signature**

```typescript
(schemaType: SchemaType, data: unknown) => ValidationResult
```

**Parameters**

| Name         | Type         | Description                      |
| ------------ | ------------ | -------------------------------- |
| `schemaType` | `SchemaType` | Which schema to validate against |
| `data`       | `unknown`    | The data to validate             |

**Returns** — Validation result with errors if invalid


**Parameters**

| Name   | Type      | Description             |
| ------ | --------- | ----------------------- |
| `task` | `unknown` | Task object to validate |

## encrypt(plaintext, projectPath)

Encrypt a plaintext string using AES-256-GCM with a per-project key.  Output format: base64(version + iv + ciphertext + authTag)   - version: 1 byte (0x01 = AES-256-GCM)   - iv: 12 bytes   - ciphertext: variable length   - authTag: 16 bytes

**Signature**

```typescript
(plaintext: string, projectPath: string) => Promise<string>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type     | Description                                                       |
| ------------- | -------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `plaintext`   | `string` | The string to encrypt (e.g. an API key).                          |
| `projectPath` | `string` | Absolute path to the project directory (used for key derivation). |

**Returns** — Base64-encoded ciphertext.

## decrypt(ciphertext, projectPath)

Decrypt a base64-encoded ciphertext using AES-256-GCM with a per-project key.

**Signature**

```typescript
(ciphertext: string, projectPath: string) => Promise<string>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type     | Description                                                                      |
| ------------- | -------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `ciphertext`  | `string` | Base64-encoded string from `encrypt()`.                                          |
| `projectPath` | `string` | Absolute path to the project directory (must match the one used for encryption). |

**Returns** — The original plaintext string.

**Throws**

- If decryption fails (wrong key, corrupted data, or machine key mismatch).

## ApprovalManager

Manages approval tokens for CANT workflow gates.  Tokens are stored in-memory per instance. In production, these are persisted via the session's `approvalTokensJson` column in tasks.db.

**Signature**

```typescript
typeof ApprovalManager
```

**Methods**

### generateToken()

Generates a new approval token for a workflow gate.

```typescript
(sessionId: string, workflowName: string, gateName: string, message: string, workflowHash: string, requestedBy: string, expiresInMs?: number) => ApprovalToken
```

### validateToken()

Validates an approval token against the current execution context.  Checks: (a) token exists, (b) sessionId matches, (c) status is pending, (d) not expired, (e) workflowHash matches current workflow.

```typescript
(tokenId: string, currentSessionId: string, currentWorkflowHash: string) => TokenValidation
```

### approveToken()

Approves a pending token.  Performs an atomic CAS transition: `pending -> approved`. If the token is not in `pending` state, the operation is a no-op and returns false.

```typescript
(tokenId: string, approvedBy: string) => boolean
```

### rejectToken()

Rejects a pending token.  Performs an atomic CAS transition: `pending -> rejected`.

```typescript
(tokenId: string) => boolean
```

### expireToken()

Expires a pending token.  Performs an atomic CAS transition: `pending -> expired`.

```typescript
(tokenId: string) => boolean
```

### getToken()

Retrieves a token by its UUID.

```typescript
(tokenId: string) => ApprovalToken | undefined
```

### getTokensForSession()

Lists all tokens for a given session.

```typescript
(sessionId: string) => ApprovalToken[]
```

### computeWorkflowHash()

Computes a SHA-256 hash of a workflow definition string.  Used for TOCTOU protection: the hash at token creation time is compared against the hash at approval time.

```typescript
(workflowText: string) => string
```

### transitionStatus()

Atomically transitions a token from `pending` to the target status.

```typescript
(tokenId: string, targetStatus: ApprovalTokenStatus) => boolean
```

## createScope(initialBindings)

Creates a new root execution scope with initial variable bindings.

**Signature**

```typescript
(initialBindings?: Record<string, unknown>) => ExecutionScope
```

**Parameters**

| Name              | Type              | Description                                              |
| ----------------- | ----------------- | -------------------------------------------------------- |
| `initialBindings` | `: Record<string` | Initial variable values (typically workflow parameters). |

**Returns** — A new root scope.

## createChildScope(parent, localBindings)

Creates a child scope that inherits from a parent.  Lookups in the child scope fall through to the parent if not found locally. This is used for parallel arms, loop iterations, and nested blocks.

**Signature**

```typescript
(parent: ExecutionScope, localBindings?: Record<string, unknown>) => ExecutionScope
```

**Parameters**

| Name            | Type              | Description                                    |
| --------------- | ----------------- | ---------------------------------------------- |
| `parent`        | `ExecutionScope`  | The parent scope.                              |
| `localBindings` | `: Record<string` | Local variable overrides for this child scope. |

**Returns** — A new child scope.

## resolveVariable(scope, name)

Resolves a variable name in the scope chain.  Searches the current scope first, then walks up the parent chain.

**Signature**

```typescript
(scope: ExecutionScope, name: string) => unknown
```

**Parameters**

| Name    | Type             | Description                   |
| ------- | ---------------- | ----------------------------- |
| `scope` | `ExecutionScope` | The scope to search in.       |
| `name`  | `string`         | The variable name to resolve. |

**Returns** — The variable value, or `undefined` if not found in any scope.

## setVariable(scope, name, value)

Sets a variable in the current scope (does not affect parent scopes).

**Signature**

```typescript
(scope: ExecutionScope, name: string, value: unknown) => void
```

**Parameters**

| Name    | Type             | Description               |
| ------- | ---------------- | ------------------------- |
| `scope` | `ExecutionScope` | The scope to modify.      |
| `name`  | `string`         | The variable name to set. |
| `value` | `unknown`        | The value to assign.      |

## resolveTemplate(template, scope)

Resolves `{variable}` placeholders in a template string against the scope.  Performs single-pass replacement per the T07 security rule: nested interpolation within resolved values is treated as literal text.

**Signature**

```typescript
(template: string, scope: ExecutionScope) => string
```

**Parameters**

| Name       | Type             | Description                                      |
| ---------- | ---------------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| `template` | `string`         | The string containing `{variable}` placeholders. |
| `scope`    | `ExecutionScope` | The execution scope for variable resolution.     |

**Returns** — The string with all placeholders resolved.

**Throws**

- Error If a referenced variable is not found in any scope.

## mergeStepOutput(scope, stepName, output)

Merges step output into the current scope.  Binds `<stepName>.stdout`, `<stepName>.stderr`, and `<stepName>.exitCode` for use in subsequent step variable resolution.

**Signature**

```typescript
(scope: ExecutionScope, stepName: string, output: Record<string, unknown>) => void
```

**Parameters**

| Name       | Type             | Description                     |
| ---------- | ---------------- | ------------------------------- |
| `scope`    | `ExecutionScope` | The scope to add bindings to.   |
| `stepName` | `string`         | The name of the completed step. |
| `output`   | `Record<string`  | The step output to merge.       |

## flattenScope(scope)

Collects all variable bindings visible from the given scope (including parents).  Parent bindings are overridden by child bindings of the same name.

**Signature**

```typescript
(scope: ExecutionScope) => Record<string, unknown>
```

**Parameters**

| Name    | Type             | Description           |
| ------- | ---------------- | --------------------- |
| `scope` | `ExecutionScope` | The scope to flatten. |

**Returns** — A flat record of all visible variable bindings.

## DefaultDiscretionEvaluator

Default discretion evaluator that always returns `true`.  This is a stub implementation. The real LLM-backed evaluator will be implemented as a separate task. In production, this should be replaced with an evaluator that: - Calls the LLM API with the condition in a structured field - Uses structured prompting (tool use / JSON mode) - Returns a boolean judgment

**Signature**


**Methods**

## RateLimitedDiscretionEvaluator

Wraps a discretion evaluator with rate limiting.  Enforces a configurable maximum number of discretion evaluations per workflow execution. Default limit is 100 per the spec. This prevents runaway costs from loops containing discretion conditions.

## sequenceChains()

Sequence two chains: connect A's exit points to B's entry point.  B's stage IDs are prefixed with "b" to avoid collision with A. The result is validated and throws if invalid.   T5406

**Signature**

```typescript
(a: WarpChain, b: WarpChain) => WarpChain
```

## parallelChains()

Compose chains in parallel with a common fork entry and join stage.  Creates a fork entry stage that links to each chain's entry, and all chain exits link to the provided joinStage.  Each chain's IDs are prefixed with "pindex" to avoid collisions.   T5406

**Signature**

```typescript
(chains: WarpChain[], joinStage: WarpStage) => WarpChain
```

## resolveEpicFromContent()

Extract an epic/task ID from file content by searching for:   1. `@task T####` or `@epic T####` annotations (highest priority)   2. JSON `"task"`, `"epicId"`, or `"taskId"` fields   3. First `T####` at a word boundary (fallback)

**Signature**

```typescript
(content: string) => string | null
```

## resolveEpicFromFilename()

Extract an epic ID from a filename pattern like `T####-*` or `T####_*`.

**Signature**

```typescript
(filename: string) => string | null
```

**Signature**

```typescript
(options?: ConsolidateOptions) => MoveRecord[]
```


## consolidateRcasd(, )

Consolidate all provenance files into the unified `.cleo/rcasd/{epicId}/` structure with stage subdirectories.  Performs migrations in order:   1. Rename suffixed directories (T4881\_install-channels → T4881)   2. Move consensus files to appropriate epic's consensus/ subdirectory   3. Move contribution files to appropriate epic's contributions/ subdirectory   4. Move loose research files to appropriate epic's research/ subdirectory

**Signature**

```typescript
(options?: ConsolidateOptions) => MigrationResult
```

**Parameters**

| Name | Type                   | Description                                                        |
| ---- | ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| ``   | `: ConsolidateOptions` | options.dryRun - If true, log planned moves without executing them |
| ``   | `: ConsolidateOptions` | options.cwd - Optional working directory override                  |

## findResumablePipelines(options, cwd)

Query active pipelines that can be resumed.  Searches the lifecycle\_pipelines table for pipelines with status 'active' and joins with lifecycle\_stages to determine current stage status. Also joins with tasks table to get task metadata.

**Signature**

```typescript
(options?: FindResumableOptions, cwd?: string) => Promise<ResumablePipeline[]>
```

**Parameters**

| Name      | Type                     | Description                    |
| --------- | ------------------------ | ------------------------------ |
| `options` | `: FindResumableOptions` | Query options for filtering    |
| `cwd`     | `: string`               | Working directory for database |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to array of resumable pipelines

**Example**

```typescript
// Find all active pipelines
const resumable = await findResumablePipelines();

// Find specific tasks
const specific = await findResumablePipelines({
  taskIds: ['T4805', 'T4806']
});

// Include blocked pipelines
const withBlocked = await findResumablePipelines({
  includeBlocked: true
});
```

## loadPipelineContext(taskId, cwd)

Load complete pipeline context for session resume.  Uses SQL JOINs to efficiently load all related data: - Pipeline and current stage - All stages with their status - Gate results for current stage - Evidence linked to current stage - Recent transitions - Task details

**Signature**

```typescript
(taskId: string, cwd?: string) => Promise<PipelineContext>
```

**Parameters**

| Name     | Type       | Description                     |
| -------- | ---------- | ------------------------------- |
| `taskId` | `string`   | The task ID to load context for |
| `cwd`    | `: string` | Working directory for database  |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to pipeline context

**Example**

```typescript
const context = await loadPipelineContext('T4805');
console.log(`Current stage: ${context.currentStage}`);
console.log(`Stage status: ${context.stages.find(s => s.stage === context.currentStage)?.status}`);
```

## resumeStage(taskId, targetStage, options, cwd)

Resume a specific stage in a pipeline.  Updates the stage status from 'blocked' or 'not\_started' to 'in\_progress', records the transition, and returns the resume result.

**Signature**

```typescript
(taskId: string, targetStage: Stage, options?: { reason?: string; agent?: string; force?: boolean; }, cwd?: string) => Promise<ResumeResult>
```

**Parameters**

| Name          | Type                                                      | Description                    |
| ------------- | --------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `taskId`      | `string`                                                  | The task ID                    |
| `targetStage` | `Stage`                                                   | The stage to resume            |
| `options`     | `: { reason?: string; agent?: string; force?: boolean; }` | Resume options                 |
| `cwd`         | `: string`                                                | Working directory for database |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to resume result

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await resumeStage('T4805', 'implement');
if (result.success) {
  console.log(`Resumed ${result.taskId} at ${result.stage}`);
}
```

## autoResume(cwd)

Auto-detect where to resume across all active pipelines.  Finds the best candidate for resuming work based on: 1. Active stages (currently in progress) 2. Blocked stages (can be unblocked) 3. Failed stages (can be retried) 4. Priority ordering

**Signature**

```typescript
(cwd?: string) => Promise<AutoResumeResult>
```

**Parameters**

| Name  | Type       | Description                    |
| ----- | ---------- | ------------------------------ |
| `cwd` | `: string` | Working directory for database |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to auto-resume result

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await autoResume();
if (result.canResume) {
  console.log(`Recommended: Resume ${result.taskId} at ${result.stage}`);
} else if (result.options && result.options.length > 0) {
  console.log('Multiple options available:', result.options);
}
```

## checkSessionResume(options, cwd)

Check for resumable work on session start.  Integrates with session initialization to check for active pipelines and present resumable work to the user. Can auto-resume if there's a clear single candidate.

**Signature**

```typescript
(options?: SessionResumeCheckOptions, cwd?: string) => Promise<SessionResumeCheckResult>
```

**Parameters**

| Name      | Type                          | Description                    |
| --------- | ----------------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `options` | `: SessionResumeCheckOptions` | Resume check options           |
| `cwd`     | `: string`                    | Working directory for database |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to resume check result

**Example**

```typescript
// On session start
const resumeCheck = await checkSessionResume({ autoResume: true });
if (resumeCheck.didResume) {
  console.log(`Auto-resumed ${resumeCheck.resumedTaskId}`);
} else if (resumeCheck.requiresUserChoice) {
  console.log('Multiple options:', resumeCheck.options);
}
```

## checkPrerequisites(targetStage, currentStages)

Check if prerequisites are met for a stage.  Validates that all prerequisite stages are in an acceptable state (completed or skipped) for the target stage to proceed.

**Signature**

```typescript
(targetStage: Stage, currentStages: Record<Stage, StageState>) => Promise<PrereqCheck>
```

**Parameters**

| Name            | Type           | Description                          |
| --------------- | -------------- | ------------------------------------ |
| `targetStage`   | `Stage`        | The stage to check prerequisites for |
| `currentStages` | `Record<Stage` | Current state of all stages          |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to PrereqCheck result

**Throws**

- CleoError If validation fails

**Example**

```typescript
const check = await checkPrerequisites('implement', {
  research: { status: 'completed' },
  spec: { status: 'completed' },
  decompose: { status: 'completed' },
  // ... other stages
});
if (check.met) {
  console.log('Ready to implement');
}
```

## validateTransition(transition, context)

Validate a stage transition.  Comprehensive validation that checks both transition rules and prerequisites. This is the core state machine validation logic.

**Signature**

```typescript
(transition: StateTransition, context: StateMachineContext) => Promise<TransitionValidation>
```

**Parameters**

| Name         | Type                  | Description                   |
| ------------ | --------------------- | ----------------------------- |
| `transition` | `StateTransition`     | The transition to validate    |
| `context`    | `StateMachineContext` | Current state machine context |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to TransitionValidation

**Throws**

- CleoError If validation fails unexpectedly

**Example**

```typescript
const validation = await validateTransition(
  { from: 'spec', to: 'implement', initiatedBy: 'agent-001' },
  pipelineContext
);
if (!validation.valid) {
  console.log(validation.errors);
}
```

## executeTransition(transition, context)

Execute a state transition.  Applies the transition to the state machine context, updating stage statuses and returning the new state. This function does NOT persist to database - that is handled by the pipeline module.

**Signature**

```typescript
(transition: StateTransition, context: StateMachineContext) => Promise<StateTransitionResult>
```

**Parameters**

| Name         | Type                  | Description                   |
| ------------ | --------------------- | ----------------------------- |
| `transition` | `StateTransition`     | The transition to execute     |
| `context`    | `StateMachineContext` | Current state machine context |

**Returns** — Promise resolving to StateTransitionResult

**Throws**

- CleoError If transition is invalid

**Example**

```typescript
const result = await executeTransition(
  { from: 'spec', to: 'implement', initiatedBy: 'agent-001' },
  pipelineContext
);
if (result.success) {
  console.log(`Transitioned to ${result.newState.stage}`);
}
```

## isValidStatusTransition(from, to)

Check if a status transition is valid.  State transitions:   not\_started → in\_progress, skipped   in\_progress → completed, blocked, failed   blocked     → in\_progress   failed      → in\_progress (retry)   completed   → (no transition - use force to override)   skipped     → (no transition)

**Signature**

```typescript
(from: StageStatus, to: StageStatus) => { valid: boolean; reason?: string; }
```

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type          | Description    |
| ------ | ------------- | -------------- |
| `from` | `StageStatus` | Current status |
| `to`   | `StageStatus` | Target status  |

**Returns** — Object with valid flag and reason   T4800

## EmbeddingQueue

Singleton embedding queue.  Batches embedding requests and processes them via a worker thread, keeping heavy model inference off the main event loop.  Use `getEmbeddingQueue` to obtain the shared instance.

**Signature**

```typescript
typeof EmbeddingQueue
```

**Methods**

### initWorker()

Initialise the worker thread if possible. Called lazily on first enqueue.

```typescript
() => Promise<void>
```

### enqueue()

Add an observation to the embedding queue.  The observation must already be persisted in brain\_observations before calling this method. `onComplete` is called asynchronously with the generated vector once the worker finishes.

```typescript
(observationId: string, text: string, onComplete: (observationId: string, embedding: Float32Array) => Promise<void>) => void
```

### scheduleDrain()

Schedule the next drain cycle via setImmediate.

```typescript
() => void
```

### drain()

Process up to `BATCH_SIZE` items from the queue. Uses the worker thread when available, falls back to inline setImmediate.

```typescript
() => Promise<void>
```

### fallbackEmbed()

Inline fallback embedding — used when worker thread is unavailable. Runs directly on the main thread (but inside setImmediate to yield first).

```typescript
(item: QueueItem) => Promise<void>
```

### shutdown()

Flush the queue and terminate the worker thread.  Waits for in-flight worker messages to drain, then terminates. Safe to call multiple times — subsequent calls return the same promise.

```typescript
() => Promise<void>
```

### doShutdown()

```typescript
() => Promise<void>
```

## getEmbeddingQueue()

Get or create the shared EmbeddingQueue singleton.  Registers a process `exit` handler on first call to flush and terminate the worker thread cleanly.

**Signature**

```typescript
() => EmbeddingQueue
```

**Returns** — The shared EmbeddingQueue instance.

## resetEmbeddingQueue()

Reset the singleton (for testing only). Shuts down the existing queue before clearing the reference.

**Signature**

```typescript
() => Promise<void>
```

## topologicalSortTasks()

Topological sort for task import order using Kahn's algorithm.  Ensures tasks are imported in dependency order: - Parents before children (parentId references) - Dependencies before dependents (depends\[] references) - Only counts edges to tasks within the set (external deps ignored)   T4552

**Signature**

```typescript
(tasks: SortableTask[]) => string[]
```

## detectCycles()

Detect cycles in task dependency graph. Returns true if no cycles, false if cycles detected.  T4552

**Signature**

```typescript
(tasks: SortableTask[]) => boolean
```

## activateStage(stageId, startedAt, cwd)

Update a stage's status to 'in\_progress' and clear block fields.

**Signature**

```typescript
(stageId: string, startedAt: string, cwd?: string) => Promise<void>
```

**Parameters**

| Name        | Type       | Description                              |
| ----------- | ---------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| `stageId`   | `string`   | Stage ID to update                       |
| `startedAt` | `string`   | ISO timestamp for when the stage started |
| `cwd`       | `: string` | Working directory for database           |

## findPipelineWithCurrentStage(taskId, cwd)

```typescript

```

| -------- | ---------- | ------------------------------ |

| `cwd`    | `: string` | Working directory for database |

## checkAtomicity()

Check task atomicity using 6-point heuristic test. Default threshold: 4 (passing requires = 4/6 criteria met).

**Signature**

```typescript
(task: Task, threshold?: number) => AtomicityResult
```

## extractTaskRefs()

Extract task IDs from text content. Scans for patterns like T1234, T001, T42 (T followed by 3+ digits).

**Signature**

```typescript
(text: string, excludeId?: string) => string[]
```

## createRelatesEntries()

Create relates entries from extracted task IDs.

**Signature**

```typescript
(refs: string[], relType?: RelatesType, reason?: string) => RelatesEntry[]
```

## mergeRelatesArrays()

Merge new relates entries with existing ones. Existing entries take precedence (dedup by taskId).

**Signature**

```typescript
(existing: RelatesEntry[], newEntries: RelatesEntry[]) => RelatesEntry[]
```

## validateRelatesRefs()

Validate that referenced task IDs exist. Returns array of invalid (non-existent) task IDs.

**Signature**

```typescript
(relates: RelatesEntry[], validTaskIds: string[]) => string[]
```

## extractAndCreateRelates()

Convenience: extract task refs from text and create relates entries.

**Signature**

```typescript
(text: string, excludeId?: string, relType?: RelatesType, reason?: string) => RelatesEntry[]
```

## calculateAffectedTasks()

Calculate which tasks would be affected by a delete operation.

**Signature**

```typescript
(taskId: string, strategy: string, tasks: Task[]) => AffectedTasks
```

## calculateImpact()

Calculate impact of deletion.

**Signature**

```typescript
(affected: AffectedTasks, tasks: Task[]) => DeleteImpact
```

## generateWarnings()

Generate warnings based on impact analysis.

**Signature**

```typescript
(affected: AffectedTasks, impact: DeleteImpact, strategy: string) => DeleteWarning[]
```

## previewDelete()

Main preview function - coordinates all preview calculations.

**Signature**

```typescript
(taskId: string, tasks: Task[], options?: { strategy?: string; reason?: string; }) => DeletePreview
```

Validate a strategy name.

**Signature**

```typescript
(strategy: string) => strategy is ChildStrategy
```

## handleChildren()

Handle children using the specified strategy. Returns the modified tasks array and the strategy result.

**Signature**

```typescript
(taskId: string, strategy: ChildStrategy, tasks: Task[], options?: { force?: boolean; cascadeThreshold?: number; allowCascade?: boolean; }) => { tasks: Task[]; result: StrategyResult; }
```

## GraphCache

Graph cache for expensive dependency calculations. Automatically invalidates when tasks change.

**Signature**

```typescript
typeof GraphCache
```

**Methods**

### computeChecksum()

Compute a simple checksum from task data to detect changes.

```typescript
(tasks: Task[]) => string
```

### isValid()

Check if cache is still valid for given tasks.

```typescript
(tasks: Task[]) => boolean
```

### isExpired()

Check if a cache entry has expired.

```typescript
<T>(entry: CacheEntry<T>) => boolean
```

### invalidate()

Invalidate all caches.

```typescript
() => void
```

### ensureFresh()

Ensure cache is fresh for the given task set.

```typescript
(tasks: Task[]) => void
```

### getDescendants()

Get descendants of a task (cached).

```typescript
(taskId: string, tasks: Task[]) => string[]
```

### getChildren()

Get children of a task (cached).

```typescript
(taskId: string, tasks: Task[]) => string[]
```

### getDependents()

Get dependents of a task (cached).

```typescript
(taskId: string, tasks: Task[]) => string[]
```

### getWaves()

Get dependency waves (cached).

```typescript
(tasks: Task[]) => DependencyWave[]
```

### getStats()

Get cache statistics.

```typescript
() => { descendantsSize: number; childrenSize: number; dependentsSize: number; hasWaves: boolean; }
```

## discoverByDescription()

**Signature**

```typescript
(taskId: string, tasks: Task[]) => DiscoveryMatch[]
```

## discoverByFiles()

Discover related tasks by shared files.

**Signature**


## discoverByHierarchy()

**Signature**

```typescript

```

## discoverRelatedTasks()

Discover related tasks using all methods combined.

**Signature**


## suggestRelates()

**Signature**

```typescript

```
